Summary:
 - For reliable benchmarking and consistent measurements, a proper OS configuration is crucial. However, the effectiveness can vary across different operating systems.
 - This includes:
   - Setting CPU isolation
   - Disabling address space layout randomization (ASLR)
   - Disabling turbo boost mode
   - Setting the CPU governor to performance
   - Disabling CPU hyper-threading
WARNING: The current configuration has been tested on a Debian-based Linux distribution (e.g., Ubuntu).
